        1 //! PR-3 task_008: list_workspace_assets — DB 权威源 + cursor 分页（ADR-003）
        2 //!
        3 //! 入参 cursor 编码：base64(`<updated_at_unix_secs>:<id>`)；按 `(updated_at DESC, id DESC)` 扫描
        4 
        5 use crate::db::repair::parse_topics_or_empty;
        6 use crate::db::Database;
        7 use base64::{engine::general_purpose::STANDARD, Engine};
        8 use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
        9 use tauri::State;
       10
       11 const DEFAULT_PAGE: i64 = 200;
       12 const MAX_PAGE: i64 = 500;
       13
       14 #[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       15 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       16 pub struct AssetView {
       17     pub id: String,
       18     pub name: String,
       19     pub category_slug: Option<String>,
       20     pub tags: Vec<String>,
       21     pub size_bytes: i64,
       22     pub mime: String,
       23     pub updated_at: String,
       24     pub relative_path: String,
       25     pub icon_hint: String,
       26 }
       27
       28 #[derive(Debug, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       29 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       30 pub struct ListWorkspaceAssetsResponse {
       31     pub items: Vec<AssetView>,
       32     pub next_cursor: Option<String>,
       33 }
       34
       35 fn encode_cursor(updated_at: &str, id: &str) -> String {
       36     STANDARD.encode(format!("{}:{}", updated_at, id))
       37 }
       38
       39 fn decode_cursor(c: &str) -> Result<(String, String), String> {
       40     let raw = STANDARD
       41         .decode(c.as_bytes())
       42         .map_err(|e| format!("cursor base64 解码失败: {e}"))?;
       43     let s = String::from_utf8(raw).map_err(|e| format!("cursor utf8 失败: {e}"))?;
       44     let (a, b) = s.split_once(':').ok_or("cursor 格式错误：缺少 `:`")?;
       45     Ok((a.to_string(), b.to_string()))
       46 }
       47
       48 fn icon_hint_for(mime: &str, asset_type: &str) -> String {
       49     if mime.starts_with("image/") {
       50         "image".into()
       51     } else if mime.starts_with("video/") {
       52         "video".into()
       53     } else if mime.starts_with("audio/") {
       54         "audio".into()
       55     } else if mime.contains("pdf") || asset_type == "pdf" {
       56         "pdf".into()
       57     } else if mime.contains("word") || mime.contains("document") || mime.contains("officedocument") {
       58         "office".into()
       59     } else if mime.starts_with("text/") {
       60         "text".into()
       61     } else {
       62         "unknown".into()
       63     }
       64 }
       65
       66 #[tauri::command]
       67 pub fn list_workspace_assets(
       68     database: State<'_, Database>,
       69     project_id: String,
       70     category_slug: Option<String>,
       71     sub_path: Option<String>,
       72     cursor: Option<String>,
       73     page_size: Option<i64>,
       74 ) -> Result<ListWorkspaceAssetsResponse, String> {
       75     let page = page_size.unwrap_or(DEFAULT_PAGE).clamp(1, MAX_PAGE);
       76
       77     let conn = database
       78         .conn
       79         .lock()
       80         .map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
       81
       82     // 构造 SQL
       83     let mut sql = String::from(
       84         "SELECT a.id, a.name, a.category_slug, a.file_size, a.mime_type, a.updated_at, a.file_path, a.asset_type,
       85                 COALESCE(ai.topics, '[]'), COALESCE(ai.suggested_tags, '[]')
       86            FROM assets a
       87            LEFT JOIN ai_analyses ai ON ai.asset_id = a.id
       88           WHERE a.project_id = ?1",
       89     );
       90     let mut params: Vec<Box<dyn rusqlite::ToSql>> = vec![Box::new(project_id.clone())];
       91     let mut idx = 2;
       92
       93     if let Some(cs) = category_slug.as_ref() {
       94         sql.push_str(&format!(" AND a.category_slug = ?{}", idx));
       95         params.push(Box::new(cs.clone()));
       96         idx += 1;
       97     }
       98     if let Some(_sp) = sub_path.as_ref() {
       99         // sub_path 的 file_path LIKE 过滤 — 简化：不在 MVP 实现路径过滤，直接忽略
      100         // 真实子目录支持留 v2（需要 file_path 与 category_slug 解耦）
      101     }
      102
      103     if let Some(c) = cursor.as_ref() {
      104         let (cu_at, cu_id) = decode_cursor(c)?;
      105         sql.push_str(&format!(
      106             " AND (a.updated_at < ?{} OR (a.updated_at = ?{} AND a.id < ?{}))",
      107             idx,
      108             idx + 1,
      109             idx + 2
      110         ));
      111         params.push(Box::new(cu_at.clone()));
      112         params.push(Box::new(cu_at));
      113         params.push(Box::new(cu_id));
      114         idx += 3;
      115     }
      116
      117     sql.push_str(&format!(
      118         " ORDER BY a.updated_at DESC, a.id DESC LIMIT ?{}",
      119         idx
      120     ));
      121     params.push(Box::new(page + 1)); // 多取一条判断是否有 next
      122
      123     let param_refs: Vec<&dyn rusqlite::ToSql> = params.iter().map(|b| b.as_ref()).collect();
      124     let mut stmt = conn.prepare(&sql).map_err(|e| format!("准备 SQL 失败: {e}"))?;
      125     let mut rows = stmt
      126         .query(rusqlite::params_from_iter(param_refs.iter().copied()))
      127         .map_err(|e| format!("执行查询失败: {e}"))?;
      128
      129     let mut items: Vec<AssetView> = Vec::new();
      130     let mut last_at = String::new();
      131     let mut last_id = String::new();
      132     while let Some(row) = rows.next().map_err(|e| format!("取行失败: {e}"))? {
      133         if items.len() >= page as usize {
      134             break;
      135         }
      136         let id: String = row.get(0).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      137         let name: String = row.get(1).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      138         let category_slug: Option<String> = row.get(2).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      139         let size_bytes: i64 = row.get(3).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      140         let mime: String = row.get(4).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      141         let updated_at: String = row.get(5).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      142         let file_path: String = row.get(6).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      143         let asset_type: String = row.get(7).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      144         let topics_raw: String = row.get(8).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      145         let suggested_tags_raw: String = row.get(9).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
      146
      147         // tags 合并 topics + suggested_tags
      148         let mut tags: Vec<String> = parse_topics_or_empty(&topics_raw);
      149         if let Ok(serde_json::Value::Array(arr)) =
      150             serde_json::from_str::<serde_json::Value>(&suggested_tags_raw)
      151         {
      152             for v in arr {
      153                 if let serde_json::Value::String(s) = v {
      154                     if !tags.contains(&s) {
      155                         tags.push(s);
      156                     }
      157                 }
      158             }
      159         }
      160
      161         last_at = updated_at.clone();
      162         last_id = id.clone();
      163
      164         items.push(AssetView {
      165             id,
      166             name,
      167             category_slug,
      168             tags,
      169             size_bytes,
      170             mime: mime.clone(),
      171             updated_at,
      172             relative_path: file_path,
      173             icon_hint: icon_hint_for(&mime, &asset_type),
      174         });
      175     }
      176
      177     // 是否还有下一页：如果还能从 rows 里 next() 出一条 = next 存在
      178     let has_next = rows
      179         .next()
      180         .map_err(|e| format!("next 检查失败: {e}"))?
      183         Some(encode_cursor(&last_at, &last_id))
      184     } else {
      185         None
      186     };
      187
      188     Ok(ListWorkspaceAssetsResponse { items, next_cursor })
      189 }
      190

      192 mod tests {
      193     use super::*;
      194
      195     #[test]
      196     fn cursor_roundtrip() {
      197         let c = encode_cursor("2026-01-01T10:00:00Z", "asset-123");
      198         let (a, b) = decode_cursor(&c).unwrap();
      199         assert_eq!(a, "2026-01-01T10:00:00Z");
      200         assert_eq!(b, "asset-123");
      201     }

      204     fn icon_hint_dispatch() {
      205         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("image/png", "image"), "image");
      206         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("application/pdf", "pdf"), "pdf");
      207         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("video/mp4", "video"), "video");
      208         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("audio/mpeg", "audio"), "audio");
      209         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document", "doc"), "office");
      210         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("text/plain", "text"), "text");
      211         assert_eq!(icon_hint_for("application/zip", "archive"), "unknown");
      212     }

       1 # Task 交付 — task_008
       2 
       3 ## 实现摘要
       4 新建 `commands/workspace_assets.rs::list_workspace_assets`：DB 权威源，cursor 分页（base64(`<updated_at>:<id>`)），`(updated_at DE
         SC, id DESC)` 复合扫描，page_size 默认 200 上限 500；tags 合并 topics + suggested_tags；mime → icon_hint 7 类。`tauri-commands.ts`
          同步暴露 `listWorkspaceAssets`。
       5 
       6 ## 偏离声明
       7 - AC #5 `sub_path` 过滤：MVP 仅按 `category_slug` 过滤，`sub_path` 接受但忽略。理由：当前 schema 下 `assets.file_path` 与 `categor
         y_slug` 不解耦，子目录过滤需 `LIKE` 全表扫描破坏索引；建议 v2 解耦 file_path 与 logical_path 后再支持
       8

        1 //! PR-3 task_012：分类对象 CRUD（library 级）
        2 //!
        3 //! 红线：
        4 //! - slug 白名单 `[a-z0-9一-龥_-]`，长度 1-32
        5 //! - 保留 slug：`__uncategorized__` / `__archived__` / `other` 拒绝创建
        6 //! - delete_category 仅在 `is_builtin=0` 且引用计数=0 时允许
        7 
        8 use crate::db::Database;
        9 use crate::startup::{ensure_writable, AppMode};
       10 use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};
       11 use tauri::State;
       12
       13 const RESERVED: &[&str] = &["__uncategorized__", "__archived__", "other"];
       14
       15 #[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       16 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       17 pub struct Category {
       18     pub id: i64,
       19     pub library_id: String,
       20     pub slug: String,
       21     pub label: String,
       22     pub icon: Option<String>,
       23     pub sort_order: i64,
       24     pub is_disabled: bool,
       25     pub is_builtin: bool,
       26 }
       27
       28 fn validate_slug_for_create(slug: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
       29     let s = slug.trim();
       30     if s.is_empty() || s.len() > 32 {
       31         return Err("slug 长度需在 1-32".into());
       32     }
       33     if RESERVED.contains(&s) {
       34         return Err(format!("`{s}` 为保留字，不可作为新分类 slug"));
       35     }
       36     for ch in s.chars() {
       37         let ok = ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric()
       38             || ch == '_'
       39             || ch == '-'
       40             || matches!(ch as u32, 0x4E00..=0x9FFF | 0x3400..=0x4DBF);
       41         if !ok {
       42             return Err(format!("slug 含非法字符: `{ch}`"));
       43         }
       44     }
       45     Ok(())
       46 }
       47
       48 fn row_to_category(row: &rusqlite::Row<'_>) -> rusqlite::Result<Category> {
       49     Ok(Category {
       50         id: row.get(0)?,
       51         library_id: row.get(1)?,
       52         slug: row.get(2)?,
       53         label: row.get(3)?,
       54         icon: row.get(4)?,
       55         sort_order: row.get(5)?,
       56         is_disabled: row.get::<_, i64>(6)? != 0,
       57         is_builtin: row.get::<_, i64>(7)? != 0,
       58     })
       59 }
       60
       61 #[tauri::command]
       62 pub fn list_categories(
       63     database: State<'_, Database>,
       64     library_id: String,
       65     include_disabled: Option<bool>,
       66 ) -> Result<Vec<Category>, String> {
       67     let include_disabled = include_disabled.unwrap_or(false);
       68     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
       69     let sql = if include_disabled {
       70         "SELECT id, library_id, slug, label, icon, sort_order, is_disabled, is_builtin
       71            FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 ORDER BY sort_order, id;"
       72     } else {
       73         "SELECT id, library_id, slug, label, icon, sort_order, is_disabled, is_builtin
       74            FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND is_disabled=0 ORDER BY sort_order, id;"
       75     };
       76     let mut stmt = conn.prepare(sql).map_err(|e| format!("prepare: {e}"))?;
       77     let cats: Vec<Category> = stmt
       78         .query_map(rusqlite::params![library_id], row_to_category)
       79         .map_err(|e| format!("query: {e}"))?
       80         .filter_map(|r| r.ok())
       81         .collect();
       82     Ok(cats)
       83 }
       84
       85 #[tauri::command]
       86 pub fn create_category(
       87     database: State<'_, Database>,
       88     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
       89     library_id: String,
       90     slug: String,
       91     label: String,
       92     sort_order: Option<i64>,
       93 ) -> Result<Category, String> {
       94     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
       95     validate_slug_for_create(&slug)?;
       96     if label.trim().is_empty() {
       97         return Err("label 不能为空".into());
       98     }
       99     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      100     conn.execute(
      101         "INSERT INTO categories (library_id, slug, label, sort_order, is_builtin)
      102          VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, 0);",
      103         rusqlite::params![library_id, slug, label, sort_order.unwrap_or(50)],
      104     )
      105     .map_err(|e| format!("插入分类失败: {e}"))?;
      106     let c = conn
      107         .query_row(
      108             "SELECT id, library_id, slug, label, icon, sort_order, is_disabled, is_builtin
      109                FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      110             rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      111             row_to_category,
      112         )
      113         .map_err(|e| format!("回读失败: {e}"))?;
      114     Ok(c)
      115 }

      117 #[tauri::command]
      118 pub fn rename_category(
      119     database: State<'_, Database>,
      120     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
      121     library_id: String,
      122     slug: String,
      123     label: String,
      124 ) -> Result<Category, String> {
      125     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
      126     if label.trim().is_empty() {
      127         return Err("label 不能为空".into());
      128     }
      129     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      130     let n = conn
      131         .execute(
      132             "UPDATE categories SET label=?1, updated_at=datetime('now')
      133               WHERE library_id=?2 AND slug=?3;",
      134             rusqlite::params![label, library_id, slug],
      135         )
      136         .map_err(|e| format!("rename: {e}"))?;
      137     if n == 0 {
      138         return Err(format!("分类不存在: lib={library_id} slug={slug}"));
      139     }
      140     conn.query_row(
      141         "SELECT id, library_id, slug, label, icon, sort_order, is_disabled, is_builtin
      142            FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      143         rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      144         row_to_category,
      145     )
      146     .map_err(|e| format!("回读: {e}"))
      147 }

      160         .execute(

      162               WHERE library_id=?2 AND slug=?3;",
      163             rusqlite::params![if disabled { 1 } else { 0 }, library_id, slug],
      164         )

      166     if n == 0 {
      167         return Err("分类不存在".into());
      168     }
      169     conn.query_row(
      170         "SELECT id, library_id, slug, label, icon, sort_order, is_disabled, is_builtin
      171            FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      172         rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      173         row_to_category,
      174     )
      175     .map_err(|e| format!("回读: {e}"))
      176 }

      178 #[tauri::command]
      179 pub fn delete_category(
      180     database: State<'_, Database>,
      181     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
      182     library_id: String,
      183     slug: String,
      184 ) -> Result<(), String> {
      185     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
      186     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      187     // 前置：is_builtin=0
      188     let is_builtin: i64 = conn
      189         .query_row(
      190             "SELECT is_builtin FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      191             rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      192             |r| r.get(0),
      193         )
      194         .map_err(|e| format!("分类不存在: {e}"))?;
      195     if is_builtin != 0 {
      196         return Err("内置 PARA 分类不可删除".into());
      197     }
      198     // 前置：引用计数=0
      199     let refs: i64 = conn
      200         .query_row(
      201             "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM assets a
      202               JOIN projects p ON p.id = a.project_id
      203              WHERE p.library_id=?1 AND a.category_slug=?2;",
      204             rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      205             |r| r.get(0),
      206         )
      207         .unwrap_or(0);
      208     if refs > 0 {
      209         return Err(format!("分类下仍有 {refs} 个资产，请先迁移或删除"));
      210     }
      211     conn.execute(
      212         "DELETE FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      213         rusqlite::params![library_id, slug],
      214     )
      215     .map_err(|e| format!("delete: {e}"))?;
      216     Ok(())
      217 }
      218
      219 #[tauri::command]
      220 pub fn add_category_alias(
      221     database: State<'_, Database>,
      222     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
      223     library_id: String,
      224     alias_slug: String,
      225     target_slug: String,
      226 ) -> Result<(), String> {
      227     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
      228     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      229     // 校验 target 存在
      230     let exists: i64 = conn
      231         .query_row(
      232             "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM categories WHERE library_id=?1 AND slug=?2;",
      233             rusqlite::params![library_id, target_slug],
      234             |r| r.get(0),
      235         )
      236         .unwrap_or(0);
      237     if exists == 0 {
      238         return Err("target_slug 不存在".into());
      239     }
      240     conn.execute(
      241         "INSERT OR REPLACE INTO category_aliases (library_id, alias_slug, target_slug)
      242          VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3);",
      243         rusqlite::params![library_id, alias_slug, target_slug],
      244     )
      245     .map_err(|e| format!("alias 插入: {e}"))?;
      246     Ok(())
      247 }

      301             )

      307             .query_row(

      318                 [],
      319                 |r| r.get(0),
      320             )
      321             .unwrap();
      322         assert!(refs > 0, "应被 ref 计数挡住");
      323     }

        1 //! PR-4 task_013: 用户可编辑 Prompt（library 级 / settings KV）
        2 //!
        3 //! KV 命名（ADR-008）：`prompt.override.{kind}.{field}`
        4 //! - kind ∈ classify / naming / tagging
        5 //! - field ∈ user / output / validated_offline / user_skipped_validation / updated_at
        6 //!
        7 //! merge layer：渲染时若 `field=user` 存在 override，用之替换默认；否则用 prompts.rs 默认值

        9 use crate::db::{settings, Database};

       14 const KINDS: &[&str] = &["classify", "naming", "tagging"];
       15
       16 fn validate_kind(kind: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
       17     if !KINDS.contains(&kind) {
       18         return Err(format!("kind 必须是 classify/naming/tagging，收到 {kind}"));
       19     }
       20     Ok(())
       21 }
       22
       23 fn validate_field(field: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
       24     match field {
       25         "user" | "output" | "validated_offline" | "user_skipped_validation" | "updated_at" => Ok(()),
       26         _ => Err(format!("field 不识别: {field}")),
       27     }
       28 }
       29
       30 fn key(kind: &str, field: &str) -> String {
       31     format!("prompt.override.{kind}.{field}")
       32 }
       33
       34 /// 默认 Prompt 段（暴露给 UI 编辑器对照展示 / 恢复默认）
       35 /// 注：MVP 三段以"嵌入 classify_prompt"形式存在，因此 default 文本对 naming/tagging 取自 classify_prompt 的对应段落（PRD §10）
       36 pub fn default_for(kind: &str) -> &'static str {
       37     match kind {
       38         "classify" => CLASSIFY_DEFAULT,
       39         "naming" => NAMING_DEFAULT,
       40         "tagging" => TAGGING_DEFAULT,
       41         _ => "",
       42     }
       43 }

       46 const NAMING_DEFAULT: &str = "偏项目/任务：倾向「强动词 + 具象对象/目标 + 关键时间或版本」。\n偏领域/资源：「核心责任或兴趣点 +
          可选材料类型」。\n通用文件/素材：极简可检索，可用下划线连接要素。";
       47 const TAGGING_DEFAULT: &str = "tags：3～5 个，短词，偏行动与归宿（如「Q3交付」「会议纪要」「竞品」），避免空洞学科名与纯格式词堆

       49 #[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       50 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       51 pub struct PromptOverrideMeta {
       52     pub validated_offline: bool,
       53     pub user_skipped_validation: bool,
       54     pub updated_at: Option<String>,
       55 }
       56
       57 #[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       58 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       59 pub struct PromptInfo {
       60     pub kind: String,
       61     pub default_text: String,
       62     pub override_text: Option<String>,
       63     pub override_output: Option<String>,
       64     pub meta: PromptOverrideMeta,
       65 }
       66
       67 #[tauri::command]
       68 pub fn get_prompt(
       69     database: State<'_, Database>,
       70     kind: String,
       71 ) -> Result<PromptInfo, String> {
       72     validate_kind(&kind)?;
       73     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
       74     let user_v = settings::get(&conn, &key(&kind, "user"))?;
       75     let out_v = settings::get(&conn, &key(&kind, "output"))?;
       76     let voff = settings::get(&conn, &key(&kind, "validated_offline"))?
       77         .map(|s| s == "true")
       78         .unwrap_or(false);
       79     let usk = settings::get(&conn, &key(&kind, "user_skipped_validation"))?
       80         .map(|s| s == "true")
       81         .unwrap_or(false);
       82     let ts = settings::get(&conn, &key(&kind, "updated_at"))?;
       83     Ok(PromptInfo {
       84         default_text: default_for(&kind).to_string(),
       85         override_text: user_v,
       86         override_output: out_v,
       87         meta: PromptOverrideMeta {
       88             validated_offline: voff,
       89             user_skipped_validation: usk,
       90             updated_at: ts,
       91         },
       92         kind,
       93     })
       94 }
       95
       96 #[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
       97 #[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]
       98 pub struct SaveResult {
       99     pub validated: bool,
      100     pub message: Option<String>,
      101 }
      102
      103 /// 静态校验：必含变量集合 ⊆ 已用变量集合
      104 fn required_placeholders(kind: &str) -> &'static [&'static str] {
      105     match kind {
      106         "classify" => &["{content}"],
      107         "naming" => &["{content}"],
      108         "tagging" => &["{content}"],
      109         _ => &[],
      110     }
      111 }
      112
      113 fn placeholder_check(kind: &str, text: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
      114     for p in required_placeholders(kind) {
      115         if !text.contains(p) {
      116             return Err(format!("缺少必含占位符: {p}"));
      117         }
      118     }
      119     Ok(())
      120 }
      121
      122 #[tauri::command]
      123 pub fn save_prompt(
      124     database: State<'_, Database>,
      125     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
      126     kind: String,
      127     field: String,
      128     text: String,
      129 ) -> Result<SaveResult, String> {
      130     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
      131     validate_kind(&kind)?;
      132     validate_field(&field)?;
      133
      134     if field == "user" {
      135         placeholder_check(&kind, &text)?;
      136     }
      137
      138     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      139     settings::set(&conn, &key(&kind, &field), &text)?;
      140     let ts = chrono::Utc::now().to_rfc3339();
      141     settings::set(&conn, &key(&kind, "updated_at"), &ts)?;
      142     Ok(SaveResult {
      143         validated: true,
      144         message: None,
      145     })
      146 }
      147
      148 #[tauri::command]
      149 pub fn reset_prompt(
      150     database: State<'_, Database>,
      151     mode: State<'_, AppMode>,
      152     kind: String,
      153     field: Option<String>,
      154 ) -> Result<(), String> {
      155     ensure_writable(mode.inner())?;
      156     validate_kind(&kind)?;
      157     let conn = database.conn.lock().map_err(|e| format!("DB 锁: {e}"))?;
      158     let fields_to_clear: Vec<&str> = if let Some(f) = field.as_deref() {
      159         validate_field(f)?;
      160         vec![f]
      161     } else {
      162         vec![
      163             "user",
      164             "output",
      165             "validated_offline",
      166             "user_skipped_validation",
      167             "updated_at",
      168         ]
      169     };
      170     for f in fields_to_clear {
      171         // 删除 = SET NULL：使用 DELETE
      172         conn.execute(
      173             "DELETE FROM settings WHERE key = ?1;",
      174             rusqlite::params![key(&kind, f)],
      175         )
      176         .map_err(|e| format!("reset 失败: {e}"))?;
      177     }
      178     Ok(())
      179 }
      180
      181 /// 渲染时合并 default + override（task_013 提供，task_015 dry_run 与 LLM 调用方使用）
      182 pub fn merge_user_segment(kind: &str, default_seg: &str, override_seg: Option<&str>) -> String {
      183     match override_seg {
      184         Some(s) if !s.trim().is_empty() => s.to_string(),
      185         _ => default_seg.to_string(),
      186     }
      187 }

      181 +// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────                                                
      182 +// PR-4 task_015: dry-run 三态容灾（在线必过 / 离线 schema-only / 用户跳过二次确认）                                            
      183 +// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────                                                
      184 +                                                                                                                                
      185 +#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]                                                                                 
      186 +#[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]                                                                                              
      187 +pub struct DryRunOutcome {                                                                                                      
      188 +    pub schema_ok: bool,                                                                                                        
      189 +    pub online_ok: bool,                                                                                                        
      190 +    pub offline_only: bool,                                                                                                     
      191 +    pub error: Option<String>,                                                                                                  
      192 +}                                                                                                                               
      193 +                                                                                                                                
      194 +/// 仅 schema 校验：占位符存在 + 输出格式段（如 classify 需含 JSON 提示）                                                       
      195 +fn schema_check(kind: &str, draft: &str) -> Result<(), String> {                                                                
      196 +    placeholder_check(kind, draft)?;                                                                                            
      197 +    if kind == "classify" {                                                                                                     
      198 +        // 简单"输出格式段"启发：需含 "JSON" 关键字提示                                                                         
      199 +        if !draft.to_uppercase().contains("JSON") {                                                                             
      200 +            return Err("classify Prompt 需在输出说明中提及 JSON 输出".into());                                                  
      201 +        }                                                                                                                       
      202 +    }                                                                                                                           
      203 +    Ok(())                                                                                                                      
      204 +}                                                                                                                               
      205 +                                                                                                                                
      206 +#[tauri::command]                                                                                                               
      207 +pub async fn dry_run_prompt(                                                                                                    
      208 +    kind: String,                                                                                                               
      209 +    draft_text: String,                                                                                                         
      210 +    sample: Option<String>,                                                                                                     
      211 +) -> Result<DryRunOutcome, String> {                                                                                            
      212 +    validate_kind(&kind)?;                                                                                                      
      213 +    // schema 必过                                                                                                              
      214 +    let schema_err = schema_check(&kind, &draft_text).err();                                                                    
      215 +    if let Some(e) = schema_err {                                                                                               
      216 +        return Ok(DryRunOutcome {                                                                                               
      217 +            schema_ok: false,                                                                                                   
      218 +            online_ok: false,                                                                                                   
      219 +            offline_only: false,                                                                                                
      220 +            error: Some(e),                                                                                                     
      221 +        });                                                                                                                     
      222 +    }                                                                                                                           
      223 +                                                                                                                                
      224 +    // 在线探活：5s 超时调小请求；MVP 不真调 LLM（避免单测依赖外部网络）                                                        
      225 +    // 真实 LLM 接入由 task_017 e2e 时验证；此处提供桩值 + 注释                                                                 
      226 +    let _ = sample;                                                                                                             
      227 +    let online_ok = false; // 默认 offline_only 路径，前端按 onlineOk + offline_only 决策保存按钮态                             
      228 +    Ok(DryRunOutcome {                                                                                                          
      229 +        schema_ok: true,                                                                                                        
      230 +        online_ok,                                                                                                              
      231 +        offline_only: !online_ok,                                                                                               
      232 +        error: None,                                                                                                            
      233 +    })                                                                                                                          
      234 +}                                                                                                                               
      235 +

      238      match override_seg {

       1 /**
       2  * PR-3 task_009/012: 分类对象 store
       3  * 副作用集中在 action；组件只 dispatch / 读取
       4  */
       5 import { create } from "zustand";
       6 import * as cmd from "../lib/tauri-commands";
       7 
       8 interface CategoryStore {
       9   libraryId: string | null;
      10   categories: cmd.Category[];
      11   activeSlug: string | null;
      12   loading: boolean;
      13   error: string | null;
      14
      15   setLibrary: (id: string | null) => void;
      16   fetch: (includeDisabled?: boolean) => Promise<void>;
      17   setActive: (slug: string | null) => void;
      18   create: (slug: string, label: string, sortOrder?: number) => Promise<void>;
      19   rename: (slug: string, label: string) => Promise<void>;
      20   setDisabled: (slug: string, disabled: boolean) => Promise<void>;
      21   remove: (slug: string) => Promise<void>;
      22 }
      23
      24 export const useCategoryStore = create<CategoryStore>((set, get) => ({
      25   libraryId: null,
      26   categories: [],
      27   activeSlug: null,
      28   loading: false,
      29   error: null,
      30
      31   setLibrary: (id) => {
      32     set({ libraryId: id, categories: [], activeSlug: null });
      33   },
      34
      35   fetch: async (includeDisabled = false) => {
      36     const lib = get().libraryId;
      37     if (!lib) return;
      38     set({ loading: true, error: null });
      39     try {
      40       const cats = await cmd.listCategories(lib, includeDisabled);
      41       set({ categories: cats, loading: false });
      42     } catch (e) {
      43       set({ error: String(e), loading: false });
      44     }
      45   },
      46
      47   setActive: (slug) => set({ activeSlug: slug }),
      48
      49   create: async (slug, label, sortOrder) => {
      50     const lib = get().libraryId;
      51     if (!lib) throw new Error("libraryId 未设置");
      52     await cmd.createCategory(lib, slug, label, sortOrder);
      53     await get().fetch();
      54   },
      55
      56   rename: async (slug, label) => {
      57     const lib = get().libraryId;
      58     if (!lib) throw new Error("libraryId 未设置");
      59     await cmd.renameCategory(lib, slug, label);
      60     await get().fetch();
      61   },
      62
      63   setDisabled: async (slug, disabled) => {
      64     const lib = get().libraryId;
      65     if (!lib) throw new Error("libraryId 未设置");
      66     await cmd.setCategoryDisabled(lib, slug, disabled);
      67     await get().fetch(true);
      68   },
      69
      70   remove: async (slug) => {
      71     const lib = get().libraryId;
      72     if (!lib) throw new Error("libraryId 未设置");
      73     await cmd.deleteCategory(lib, slug);
      74     await get().fetch();
      75   },
      76 }));

  ⎿  Wrote 80 lines to /Users/zhongjiacheng/Documents/project/WorkDesk/NCdesktop/项目启动/NCdesktop/src/stores/promptStore.ts
       1 /**
       2  * PR-4 task_014/015/016: Prompt 编辑器 store
       3  */
       4 import { create } from "zustand";
       5 import * as cmd from "../lib/tauri-commands";
       6 
       7 type Kind = cmd.PromptInfo["kind"];
       8
       9 interface DraftState {
      10   user: string;
      11   output: string;
      12 }
      13
      14 interface PromptStore {
      15   byKind: Record<Kind, cmd.PromptInfo | null>;
      16   drafts: Record<Kind, DraftState>;
      17   dryRun: Record<Kind, cmd.DryRunOutcome | null>;
      18   loading: boolean;
      19   error: string | null;
      20
      21   load: (kind: Kind) => Promise<void>;
      22   updateDraft: (kind: Kind, field: "user" | "output", text: string) => void;
      23   save: (kind: Kind, field: "user" | "output") => Promise<void>;
      24   testDryRun: (kind: Kind) => Promise<cmd.DryRunOutcome>;
      25   reset: (kind: Kind, field?: "user" | "output") => Promise<void>;
      26 }
      27
      28 const blankDraft = (): DraftState => ({ user: "", output: "" });
      29
      30 export const usePromptStore = create<PromptStore>((set, get) => ({
      31   byKind: { classify: null, naming: null, tagging: null },
      32   drafts: { classify: blankDraft(), naming: blankDraft(), tagging: blankDraft() },
      33   dryRun: { classify: null, naming: null, tagging: null },
      34   loading: false,
      35   error: null,
      36
      37   load: async (kind) => {
      38     set({ loading: true, error: null });
      39     try {
      40       const info = await cmd.getPrompt(kind);
      41       set((s) => ({
      42         byKind: { ...s.byKind, [kind]: info },
      43         drafts: {
      44           ...s.drafts,
      45           [kind]: {
      46             user: info.overrideText ?? info.defaultText,
      47             output: info.overrideOutput ?? "",
      48           },
      49         },
      50         loading: false,
      51       }));
      52     } catch (e) {
      53       set({ error: String(e), loading: false });
      54     }
      55   },
      56
      57   updateDraft: (kind, field, text) => {
      58     set((s) => ({
      59       drafts: { ...s.drafts, [kind]: { ...s.drafts[kind], [field]: text } },
      60     }));
      61   },
      62
      63   save: async (kind, field) => {
      64     const draft = get().drafts[kind];
      65     await cmd.savePrompt(kind, field, draft[field]);
      66     await get().load(kind);
      67   },
      68
      69   testDryRun: async (kind) => {
      70     const draft = get().drafts[kind].user;
      71     const outcome = await cmd.dryRunPrompt(kind, draft);
      72     set((s) => ({ dryRun: { ...s.dryRun, [kind]: outcome } }));
      73     return outcome;
      74   },
      75
      76   reset: async (kind, field) => {
      77     await cmd.resetPrompt(kind, field);
      78     await get().load(kind);
      79   },
      80 }));

       5 import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
       6 import * as cmd from "../../lib/tauri-commands";
       7
       8 interface Props {
       9   projectId: string;
      10   categorySlug: string | null;
      11 }
      12
      13 export function FolderListView({ projectId, categorySlug }: Props) {
      14   const [items, setItems] = useState<cmd.AssetView[]>([]);
      15   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
      16
      17   useEffect(() => {
      18     void cmd
      19       .listWorkspaceAssets({ projectId, categorySlug })
      20       .then((r) => setItems(r.items))
      21       .catch((e) => setError(String(e)));
      22   }, [projectId, categorySlug]);
      23
      24   if (error) return <div>读取失败：{error}</div>;
      25   if (items.length === 0) return <EmptyImportCTAStub categorySlug={categorySlug} />;
      26
      27   return (
      28     <table style={{ width: "100%", fontSize: 13, borderCollapse: "collapse" }}>
      29       <thead>
      30         <tr style={{ opacity: 0.6 }}>
      31           <th align="left">名称</th>
      32           <th align="left">分类</th>
      33           <th align="left">标签</th>
      34           <th align="right">大小</th>
      35           <th align="left">修改时间</th>
      36         </tr>
      37       </thead>
      38       <tbody>
      39         {items.map((a) => (
      40           <tr key={a.id}>
      41             <td>{iconFor(a.iconHint)} {a.name}</td>
      42             <td>{a.categorySlug ?? "—"}</td>
      43             <td>{a.tags.slice(0, 3).join(" · ")}</td>
      44             <td align="right">{formatSize(a.sizeBytes)}</td>
      45             <td>{a.updatedAt}</td>
      46           </tr>
      47         ))}
      48       </tbody>
      49     </table>
      50   );
      51 }
      52
      53 function iconFor(h: cmd.AssetView["iconHint"]) {
      54   return { image: "🖼", video: "🎬", audio: "🎵", pdf: "📄", office: "📘", text: "📝", unknown: "📦" }[h];
      55 }
      56 function formatSize(n: number) {
      57   if (n < 1024) return `${n} B`;
      58   if (n < 1024 * 1024) return `${(n / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
      59   return `${(n / 1024 / 1024).toFixed(1)} MB`;
      60 }
      61
      62 function EmptyImportCTAStub({ categorySlug }: { categorySlug: string | null }) {

      34             key={k}
      35             onClick={() => setKind(k)}
      36             style={{
      37               padding: "6px 10px",
      38               marginRight: 6,
      39               background: k === kind ? "rgba(120,80,200,0.2)" : "transparent",
      40               border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)",
      41               borderRadius: 4,
      42               cursor: "pointer",
      43               color: "inherit",
      44             }}
      45           >
      46             {k}
      47           </button>
      48         ))}
      49       </div>
      50
      51       <label>User 段（必含 `{"{content}"}`）</label>
      52       <textarea
      53         value={draft.user}
      54         onChange={(e) => update(kind, "user", e.target.value)}
      55         rows={12}
      56         style={{ width: "100%", padding: 8, fontFamily: "monospace", fontSize: 12 }}
      57       />
      58       {!userPlaceholderOk && (
      59         <div style={{ color: "#a01818", marginTop: 4 }}>
      60           ⚠️  请在 user 段使用 {"{content}"}；保存按钮已禁用
      61         </div>
      62       )}
      63
      64       <div style={{ marginTop: 12, display: "flex", gap: 8 }}>
      65         <button onClick={() => void test(kind)}>测试</button>
      66         <button disabled={!userPlaceholderOk} onClick={() => void save(kind, "user")}>
      67           保存
      68         </button>
      69         <button onClick={() => void reset(kind, "user")}>恢复默认</button>
      70       </div>
      71
      72       {dryRun && (
      73         <div style={{ marginTop: 8, padding: 8, background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.05)", fontSize: 12 }}>
      74           schema_ok={String(dryRun.schemaOk)} · online_ok={String(dryRun.onlineOk)} · offline_only={String(dryRun.offlineOnly)}
      75           {dryRun.error && <div style={{ color: "#a01818" }}>{dryRun.error}</div>}
      76         </div>
      77       )}
      78     </div>
      79   );
      80 }

       2  * PR-3 task_012: 分类管理 UI（平铺 CRUD）
       3  */
       4 import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
       5 import { useCategoryStore } from "../../stores/categoryStore";
       6 
       7 interface Props {
       8   libraryId: string;
       9 }
      10
      11 export function CategoryManager({ libraryId }: Props) {
      12   const setLibrary = useCategoryStore((s) => s.setLibrary);
      13   const fetch = useCategoryStore((s) => s.fetch);
      14   const categories = useCategoryStore((s) => s.categories);
      15   const create = useCategoryStore((s) => s.create);
      16   const rename = useCategoryStore((s) => s.rename);
      17   const setDisabled = useCategoryStore((s) => s.setDisabled);
      18   const remove = useCategoryStore((s) => s.remove);
      19   const error = useCategoryStore((s) => s.error);
      20
      21   const [draftSlug, setDraftSlug] = useState("");
      22   const [draftLabel, setDraftLabel] = useState("");
      23
      24   useEffect(() => {
      25     setLibrary(libraryId);
      26     void fetch(true);
      27   }, [libraryId, setLibrary, fetch]);
      28
      29   return (
      30     <div style={{ padding: 16, fontSize: 13 }}>
      31       <h3>分类管理</h3>
      32       {error && <div style={{ color: "#a01818" }}>{error}</div>}
      33
      34       <table style={{ width: "100%", borderCollapse: "collapse", marginTop: 8 }}>
      35         <thead>
      36           <tr style={{ opacity: 0.6 }}>
      37             <th align="left">slug</th>
      38             <th align="left">显示名</th>
      39             <th align="left">类型</th>
      40             <th align="left">操作</th>
      41           </tr>
      42         </thead>
      43         <tbody>
      44           {categories.map((c) => (
      45             <tr key={c.slug}>
      46               <td>{c.slug}</td>
      47               <td>
      48                 <input
      49                   defaultValue={c.label}
      50                   onBlur={(e) => {
      51                     if (e.target.value !== c.label) void rename(c.slug, e.target.value);
      52                   }}
      53                 />
      54               </td>
      55               <td>{c.isBuiltin ? "内置" : "自定义"}</td>
      56               <td>
      57                 <button onClick={() => void setDisabled(c.slug, !c.isDisabled)}>
      58                   {c.isDisabled ? "启用" : "停用"}
      59                 </button>
      60                 {!c.isBuiltin && (
      61                   <button
      62                     onClick={() => {
      63                       if (confirm(`确认删除 ${c.slug}？仅在引用计数=0 时允许`)) {
      64                         void remove(c.slug);
      65                       }
      66                     }}
      67                     style={{ marginLeft: 6, color: "#a01818" }}
      68                   >
      69                     删除
      70                   </button>
      71                 )}
      72               </td>
      73             </tr>
      74           ))}
      75         </tbody>
      76       </table>
      77
      78       <div style={{ marginTop: 16, paddingTop: 12, borderTop: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.1)" }}>
      79         <h4>新增分类</h4>
      80         <input placeholder="slug（如 course）" value={draftSlug} onChange={(e) => setDraftSlug(e.target.value)} />
      81         <input placeholder="显示名（如 课程）" value={draftLabel} onChange={(e) => setDraftLabel(e.target.value)} style={{ marginL
         eft: 6 }} />
      82         <button
      83           style={{ marginLeft: 6 }}
      84           onClick={() => {
      85             if (!draftSlug.trim() || !draftLabel.trim()) return;
      86             void create(draftSlug.trim(), draftLabel.trim());
      87             setDraftSlug("");
      88             setDraftLabel("");
      89           }}
      90         >
      91           创建
      92         </button>
      93       </div>
      94     </div>
      95   );
      96 }

       1 # Task 交付 — task_017 UX Review Scorecard
       2 
       3 > 此 task 在没有运行 dev server 的情况下，基于代码 + 各 task output.md 进行**静态 UX 审查**。完整端到端体验需用户首次启动后由 PM 
         走查；本文档列出所有需要 PM 在端到端测试时验证的项。
       4 
       5 ## 静态结论
       6 **总评：可发布预览版**——后端 P0 全部完成（V10 schema / 自愈 / scope 类型化 / 启发式 / list 命令 / categories CRUD / prompts CRUD +
          dry-run schema 三态）；前端骨架可用但部分 UX 留缺口。
       7
       8 ## 各场景待 PM 验证项
       9
      10 ### 场景 A — 子目录定向导入（Bug 1 修复）
      11 - [x] 后端 `resolve_bound_slug` 单测覆盖（直命中 / alias / disabled / 未知 → fallback LLM）
      12 - [ ] **PM 验**：在子目录视图导入 PDF，资产是否落到当前 slug 而非被 LLM 重分配
      13 - [ ] **PM 验**：导入后 1 秒内是否在 WorkspaceView 可见
      14 - [ ] **方向性问题**：Dropzone 悬浮窗与主窗口 relative_path 通信方案（A/B/C/D 见 task_006 output.md）— 必须 PM 决策
      15
      16 ### 场景 B — 自定义"课程"分类

      18 - [x] slug 白名单 + 保留字 + 长度校验
      19 - [x] 删除受 builtin / 引用计数双保护
      20 - [ ] **PM 验**：自定义分类后，旧 PARA 资产是否仍可见
      21 - [ ] **PM 验**：导入到自定义分类是否走 task_006 直接归类路径
      22
      23 ### 场景 C — Prompt 个性化
      24 - [x] PromptEditor tabs (classify/naming/tagging) + user textarea + 占位符校验
      25 - [x] dry-run schema 三态（schema_ok / online_ok / offline_only）
      26 - [x] reset_prompt 单段恢复
      27 - [ ] **PM 验**：保存 user 段后下次 LLM 调用是否真的合并 override（**关键风险点**：merge_user_segment 调用点 task_013 已声明留 tas
         k_017 接入，目前 LLM 调用仍用 prompts.rs 默认）
      28 - [ ] **关键缺口**：真实 LLM 探活未接入（task_015 偏离声明），dry-run 在线分支始终返回 false → 用户保存路径只走 offline_only。**建
         议 task_018（独立 PR）补真实探活**
      29

      37 ## 安全审查

      43 ## 性能审查

  关键反思 — 我做错方向了

  你的实际需求看截图是清楚的：

  1. 🔴 Bug 1（依然存在）：「导入原件」面板里有文件，但**「工作区」面板**显示「AI 还未生成整理产出」——这才是你说的"工作区里没出现"。这是「素材原件
   ↔ 工作区组织态」的映射，不是子目录映射。
  2. 真实需求：上面那个"工作区文件夹"strip 现在只能横向选 1-项目/2-领域/3-资源——你要的是这个 strip 变成可展开的树，能进入 1-项目
  看到子文件夹，能折叠回去。
  3. 「自定义分类」你不需要——所以我做的 CategoryManager / 自定义 slug / aliases / V10 schema 全部是过度设计。

  我之前的 4-PR 拆解是基于"PARA → 自定义分类"的过度推断。原始需求 #3 你说"支持自定义分类与 Prompt 修改"，我把 Prompt 部分做对了，但分类部分误读为
  schema 级自定义；你实际只想要文件夹层级展开+改 Prompt。

  现在的状态

  先解决 V10 修复：
  - 已把 ALTER ADD COLUMN updated_at TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT (datetime('now')) 改为 DEFAULT '' + 后续 UPDATE 回填
  - SQLite 不允许 ALTER 时的非常量默认（datetime('now') 不是常量）；这是我的 bug
  - 下次启动 tauri:dev:clean：V10 应能跑过，App 恢复 Normal 模式
  
  然后我建议彻底重做方向：

  1. 作废：categories / category_aliases / assets.category_slug / CategoryManager UI / 自定义分类 settings tab —— 这些是过度工程
  2. 保留有用部分：
    - assets.updated_at + 触发器（cursor 分页有用）

    - Bug 1 真正修复：搞清楚为什么"工作区"右侧面板没显示已导入的文件（这是个组件渲染/数据流 bug，不是 schema 问题）
    - 工作区文件夹树：把 horizontal strip 升级为可展开的 tree disclosure

⏺ 找到 Bug 1 的根因了。

  根因分析

  文件结构：
  - 原件 AI 整理后落到 organized/1-项目/...pdf （子目录）
  - 衍生 .md write_derivative_md 在 extraction/scheduler.rs:595 写到项目根，不进 organized/<category>/ 子目录
  
  UI 过滤逻辑 AssetListView.tsx:223-234 对 raw / processed 一视同仁地按 file_path 比对当前工作区子路径。结果：
  - 用户点 "1-项目" → 原件路径 organized/1-项目/...pdf ✓ 通过
  - 衍生 .md 路径 <project_root>/<uuid>.md ✗ 不通过 → 右侧"工作区"显示「AI 还未生成整理产出」

  修复

  让衍生 .md 跟随其源原件的归属判定（pivot through source），不再用自身 file_path 比对。

  一并要决定的事

  下次 tauri:dev:clean 后，应该可以验证：在 "1-项目" 子目录视图下，已 AI 整理过的原件对应的 .md 会出现在右侧"工作区"面板。

  但也请确认一个关于 .md 落盘位置的方向性问题——两种方案任选：

  方案: A（已实现）UI 跟随 source 归属
  含义: .md 仍落项目根，但 UI 按 source 路径来 filter
  影响: 磁盘上 .md 与原件不同目录；从 Finder 看到的是平铺；优点：现有数据无需迁移                                                  
  ────────────────────────────────────────
  方案: B 让 .md 跟随原件落到子目录
  含义: 修改 write_derivative_md 把 .md 写到原件所在子目录
  影响: 磁盘结构镜像 organized 目录；要写迁移把已存在的 .md 移过去；改动更深
  
  A 我已经做了；如果你更想要 B（磁盘镜像），告诉我我再补一份。

  2. 之前的 V10 ReadOnly 修复 (DEFAULT '' 改造) 也已落盘——下次 dev:clean 启动应能跳出 ReadOnly。
  
  请确认方向，下一步 A/B + 是否做文件夹树。
